# standard costs
@maa_buy_cost = 150
@maa_low_maintenance_cost = 1.0
@maa_high_maintenance_cost = 3.5
@cultural_maa_extra_ai_score = 60 # Equivalent to having 6 extra regiments beyond what the code scoring would indicate (see NEGATIVE_SCORE_PER_EXISTING_REGIMENT)

# Must be synced between files with the values located at "# Provisions Costs #".
@provisions_cost_infantry_cheap = 3
@provisions_cost_infantry_moderate = 7
@provisions_cost_infantry_expensive = 12
@provisions_cost_infantry_bankrupting = 15

@provisions_cost_cavalry_cheap = 7
@provisions_cost_cavalry_moderate = 15
@provisions_cost_cavalry_expensive = 21
@provisions_cost_cavalry_bankrupting = 30

@provisions_cost_special_cheap = 6
@provisions_cost_special_moderate = 12
@provisions_cost_special_expensive = 18
@provisions_cost_special_bankrupting = 24

accolade_maa_archers = {
	type = archers
	icon = bowmen

#	can_recruit = {
#		any_active_accolade = { 
#			primary_type = {
#				this = accolade_type:archer_attribute
#			}
#			accolade_rank >= 3
#		}
#	}

	can_recruit = { always = no }                                   ### Added
	
	damage = 30
	toughness = 15
	pursuit = 0
	screen = 0
	
	terrain_bonus = {
		hills = { damage = 20 toughness = 8 }
		forest = { toughness = 8 screen = 8 }
		taiga = { toughness = 8 screen = 8 }
	}

	counters = {
		skirmishers = 2
	}

	buy_cost = { gold = accolade_bowmen_recruitment_cost }
	low_maintenance_cost = { gold = bowmen_low_maint_cost }
	high_maintenance_cost = { gold = bowmen_high_maint_cost }
	provision_cost = @provisions_cost_infantry_cheap												 

	max_sub_regiments = 8
	
	stack = 100
	ai_quality = {
		value = culture_ai_weight_archers
		add = 50
	}
}

############################  SAXON  ############################

accolade_maa_archers_saxon = {
	type = archers
	icon = saxon_bowmen

    can_recruit = {
        culture = {
		OR = {		
			this = culture:frankish             ### Important to leave without parent trigger, because it is parent to other!

			this = culture:saxon
			any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:saxon
				}
			this = culture:old_saxon
			any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:old_saxon
				}					
            }
		NOR = {
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_akan
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_ancient_greek
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_baltic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_balto_finnic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bantu
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_brythonic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_burman
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_central_african
                ### has_cultural_pillar = heritage_central_germanic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_chinese
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dravidian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_east_african
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_east_slavic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_egyptian
				### has_cultural_pillar = heritage_frankish
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_goidelic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_gothic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_hunnic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iberian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_indo_aryan
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_magyar
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_mongolic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_north_germanic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_qiangic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_sahelian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_senegambian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_somalian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_south_slavic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tibetan
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tocharian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_turkic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_ugro_permian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_vlach
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_volga_finnic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_african
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_germanic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_slavic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_yoruba
    			has_cultural_pillar = heritage_albanian
			    has_cultural_pillar = heritage_syriac	
				this = culture:french
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
					this = culture:french
				}
				this = culture:occitan
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
					this = culture:occitan
				}
				this = culture:anglo_saxon
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
					this = culture:anglo_saxon
				}			
			}
		}			
				any_active_accolade = { 
				primary_type = {
				this = accolade_type:archer_attribute
			}
			accolade_rank >= 3
		}
	}
	
	damage = 30
	toughness = 15
	pursuit = 0
	screen = 0
	
	terrain_bonus = {
		hills = { damage = 20 toughness = 8 }
		forest = { toughness = 8 screen = 8 }
		taiga = { toughness = 8 screen = 8 }
	}

	counters = {
		skirmishers = 2
	}

	buy_cost = { gold = accolade_bowmen_recruitment_cost }
	low_maintenance_cost = { gold = bowmen_low_maint_cost }
	high_maintenance_cost = { gold = bowmen_high_maint_cost }
	provision_cost = @provisions_cost_infantry_cheap

	max_sub_regiments = 8
	
	stack = 100
	ai_quality = {
		value = culture_ai_weight_archers
		add = 50
	}
}

				this = culture:saxon		       ### anglo-saxon army is disabled for central germanic saxon	
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:saxon			
				}			
				this = culture:english
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:english	
				}
				this = culture:scottish
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:scottish	
				}
				this = culture:gaelic
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:gaelic
				}
				this = culture:pictish
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:pictish
				}
				this = culture:cumbrian
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:cumbrian
				}				
			}
		} 			
				any_active_accolade = { 
				primary_type = {
				this = accolade_type:crossbowmen_attribute
			}
				accolade_rank >= 3
		}
	}

	damage = 60
	toughness = 30
	pursuit = 0
	screen = 0
	
	terrain_bonus = {
		hills = { damage = 20 }
		plains = { toughness = -4 }
		drylands = { toughness = -4 }
		desert = { toughness = -4 }
	}

	counters = {
		heavy_infantry = 2
		heavy_cavalry = 2
		archer_cavalry = 1
	}

	buy_cost = { gold = accolade_crossbowmen_recruitment_cost }
	low_maintenance_cost = { gold = crossbowmen_low_maint_cost }
	high_maintenance_cost = { gold = crossbowmen_high_maint_cost }
	provision_cost = @provisions_cost_infantry_moderate													

	max_sub_regiments = 6
	
	stack = 100

		add = 100

	icon = scottish_heavy_cavalry

    can_recruit = {
        culture = {
			OR = {
				this = culture:scottish
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:scottish
				}
				this = culture:gaelic
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:gaelic
				}
				this = culture:pictish
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:pictish
				}
				this = culture:cumbrian
				any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:cumbrian
				}				
			}
           NOR = {
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_akan
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_ancient_greek
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_baltic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_balto_finnic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bantu
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber
                ### has_cultural_pillar = heritage_brythonic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_burman
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_central_african
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_central_germanic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_chinese
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dravidian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_east_african
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_east_slavic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_egyptian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_frankish
                ### has_cultural_pillar = heritage_goidelic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_gothic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_hunnic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iberian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_indo_aryan
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_magyar
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_mongolic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_north_germanic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_qiangic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_sahelian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_senegambian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_somalian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_south_slavic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tibetan
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tocharian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_turkic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_ugro_permian
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_vlach
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_volga_finnic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_african
                ### has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_germanic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_slavic
                has_cultural_pillar = heritage_yoruba
    			has_cultural_pillar = heritage_albanian
			    has_cultural_pillar = heritage_syriac
            }
        }
		any_active_accolade = { 
			primary_type = {
				this = accolade_type:lancer_attribute
			}
			accolade_rank >= 3
		}
	}

	damage = 200
	toughness = 70
	pursuit = 40
	screen = 0
	
	terrain_bonus = {
		plains = { damage = 60 }
		drylands = { damage = 60 }
		hills = { damage = -10 }
		mountains = { damage = -35 }
		desert_mountains = { damage = -35 }
		wetlands = { damage = -35 toughness = -5 pursuit = -5 }
	}

	counters = {
		archers = 2
	}

	winter_bonus = {
		normal_winter = { damage = -10 toughness = -5 }
		harsh_winter = { damage = -20 toughness = -10 }
	}

	buy_cost = { gold = accolade_heavy_cavalry_recruitment_cost }
	low_maintenance_cost = { gold = heavy_cavalry_low_maint_cost }
	high_maintenance_cost = { gold = heavy_cavalry_high_maint_cost }
	provision_cost = @provisions_cost_cavalry_expensive													

	max_sub_regiments = 6
	
	stack = 50
	ai_quality = {
		value = culture_ai_weight_heavy_cavalry
		add = 100
	}
}

accolade_maa_archers_french = {
	type = archers
	icon = french_bowmen

    can_recruit = {
        culture = {
		OR = {
			this = culture:french
			any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:french
			}
			this = culture:occitan
			any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:occitan
				}
			}
		NOR = {
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_akan
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_ancient_greek
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_arabic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_baltic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_balto_finnic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_bantu
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_berber
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_brythonic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_burman
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_byzantine
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_central_african
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_central_germanic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_chinese
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_dravidian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_east_african
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_east_slavic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_egyptian
            ### has_cultural_pillar = heritage_frankish
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_goidelic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_gothic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_hunnic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iberian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_indo_aryan
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_iranian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_israelite
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_latin
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_magyar
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_mongolic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_north_germanic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_qiangic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_sahelian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_senegambian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_somalian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_south_slavic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tibetan
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_tocharian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_turkic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_ugro_permian
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_vlach
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_volga_finnic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_african
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_germanic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_slavic
            has_cultural_pillar = heritage_yoruba
    			has_cultural_pillar = heritage_albanian
			    has_cultural_pillar = heritage_syriac		
			this = culture:frankish            ### Important to leave without parent trigger, because it is parent to french!
			
			this = culture:norman
			any_parent_culture_or_above = {
				this = culture:norman
				}			
            }						
        }
		any_active_accolade = { 
			primary_type = {
				this = accolade_type:archer_attribute
			}
			accolade_rank >= 3
		}
	}
	
	damage = 30
	toughness = 15
	pursuit = 0
	screen = 0
	
	terrain_bonus = {
		hills = { damage = 20 toughness = 8 }
		forest = { toughness = 8 screen = 8 }
		taiga = { toughness = 8 screen = 8 }
	}

	counters = {
		skirmishers = 2
	}

	buy_cost = { gold = accolade_bowmen_recruitment_cost }
	low_maintenance_cost = { gold = bowmen_low_maint_cost }
	high_maintenance_cost = { gold = bowmen_high_maint_cost }
	provision_cost = @provisions_cost_infantry_cheap

	max_sub_regiments = 8
	
	stack = 100
	ai_quality = {
		value = culture_ai_weight_archers
		add = 50
	}
}
